    <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Introductory Note.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">As previously disclosed in the Current Reports on Forms 8-K and 8-K/A filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;<span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;">SEC</span>&#8221;) on May 4, 2021, by Tilray, Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#8220;<span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;">Tilray</span>&#8221;), Tilray consummated a plan of arrangement <span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">under the Business Corporations Act (Ontario) (the &#8220;</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;">Arrangement</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">&#8221;) </span>with Aphria Inc., a <span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">corporation
        existing under the laws of the Province of Ontario (&#8220;</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;">Aphria</span><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">&#8221;), </span>on


      April 30, 2021.&#160; For accounting purposes, the Arrangement was treated as a reverse acquisition, and Aphria was considered the accounting acquirer. Accordingly, <a id="z_Hlk72010101"></a>following the consummation of the Arrangement, the historical
      financial statements of Aphria became the historical financial statements of Tilray.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Prior to the completion of the Arrangement, PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP (&#8220;<span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;">PwC</span>&#8221;) served as the independent registered public accounting firm of Aphria, and Deloitte LLP (&#8220;<span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;">Deloitte</span>&#8221;)


      served as the independent registered public accounting firm of Tilray.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div>
      <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" class="DSPFListTable" id="z8616fa580adc4c5cbf717c9eb43c481e" style="width: 100%; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">


  <tr style="vertical-align: top;">

    <td style="vertical-align: top; width: 63pt;">
              <div style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Item 4.01.</span></div>
            </td>

    <td style="align: left; vertical-align: top; width: auto;">
              <div style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);">Changes in Registrant&#8217;s Certifying Accountant.</span></div>
            </td>

  </tr>


</table>
    </div>

    <div><br />
    </div>

    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: rgb(0, 0, 0);" class="DSPFListTable" id="zb90a4a2aa5da4cc2bbc388a1c85ac040">


  <tr>

    <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic;">(a)</td>

    <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: justify;">
            <div style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic;">Dismissal of Independent Registered Public Accounting Firm</div>
          </td>

  </tr>


</table>
    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">On May 21, 2021, the board of directors of Tilray (the &#8220;<span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;">Board</span>&#8221;) approved the dismissal of Deloitte as Tilray&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm, and on the same day, Tilray dismissed Deloitte as its independent registered public accounting firm.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Deloitte&#8217;s audit report on Tilray&#8217;s consolidated financial statements for the fiscal years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019, did not contain an
      adverse opinion or a disclaimer of opinion, and was not qualified or modified as to uncertainties, audit scope or accounting principles.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">During the interim period from January 1, 2021 through May 21, 2021, and the fiscal years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019, there were no
      disagreements between Tilray and Deloitte on any matter of accounting principles or practices, financial disclosure or auditing scope or procedure, which disagreements, if not resolved to the satisfaction of Deloitte would have caused it to make
      reference to the subject matter of the disagreements in its report on Tilray&#8217;s financial statements for such periods.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">During the interim period from January 1, 2021 through May 21, 2021, and the fiscal years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019, there were no
      &#8220;reportable events&#8221; (as defined in Item 304(a)(1)(v) of Regulation S-K under the Securities Exchange Act on 1934, as amended), except as noted below.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic;">Fiscal 2020</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">As disclosed in Item 9A of Tilray&#8217;s Annual Report on Form 10-K for the fiscal year
        ended December 31, 2020, filed with the SEC on February 19, 2021 (as amended on April 28, 2021), </span>Deloitte expressed an adverse opinion on Tilray&#8217;s internal control over financial reporting as of December 31, 2020, due to material weaknesses
      relating to: (i) ineffective controls over the review procedures for balance sheet account reconciliations and manual journal entries; (ii) ineffective controls over the completeness and accuracy of key spreadsheets and reports used in the
      measurement and valuation of inventory; and (iii) lack of evidence of review procedures and lack of sufficient segregation of duties within the accounting function for the Portugal and Manitoba Harvest business units.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic;">Fiscal 2019</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">As disclosed in Item 9A of Tilray&#8217;s Annual Report on Form 10-K for the fiscal year
        ended December 31, 2019, filed with the SEC on March 2, 2020 (as amended on April 29, 2020), </span>Deloitte expressed an adverse opinion on Tilray&#8217;s internal control over financial reporting as of December 31, 2019, due to material weaknesses
      relating to (i) appropriate organizational structure, reporting lines, and authority and responsibilities in pursuit of objectives; (ii) Tilray&#8217;s commitment to attract, develop, and retain competent individuals; (iii) holding individuals accountable
      for their internal control related responsibilities; (iv) selecting and developing control activities that contribute to the mitigation of risks to the achievement of objectives to acceptable levels; and (v) deploying control activities through
      policies that establish what is expected and procedures that put policies into action.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The subject matter of these reportable events was discussed by the audit committee of the Board (the &#8220;<span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;">Audit Committee</span>&#8221;) with Deloitte. Tilray has authorized Deloitte to respond fully to the inquiries of Tilray&#8217;s newly appointed independent registered public accounting firm concerning
      the subject matter of the reportable events described above.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">Tilray provided Deloitte with a copy of the foregoing disclosures and requested that Deloitte furnish Tilray with a letter addressed to the SEC
      stating whether it agrees with the statements made by Tilray set forth above. A copy of Deloitte&#8217;s letter dated May 21, 2021, is filed as Exhibit 16.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

  <tr>

    <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic;">(b)</td>

    <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: justify;">
            <div style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-style: italic;">Appointment of New Independent Registered Public Accounting Firm</div>
          </td>

  </tr>


</table>
    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">On May 21, 2021, the Board, acting upon recommendation of the Audit Committee, approved the engagement of PwC, effective as of May 21, 2021, as
      Tilray&#8217;s independent registered public accounting firm for the fiscal year ended May 31, 2021 to audit Tilray&#8217;s financial statements.</div>

    <div>&#160;</div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">During the interim period from June 1, 2020 through May 21, 2021, and the fiscal years ended May 31, 2020 and 2019, neither Tilray nor anyone on its
      behalf consulted with PwC, regarding either: (i) the application of accounting principles to a specific transaction, completed or proposed, or the type of audit opinion that might be rendered on Tilray&#8217;s financial statements, and neither a written
      report nor oral advice was provided to Tilray that PwC concluded was an important factor considered by Tilray in reaching a decision as to any accounting, auditing or financial reporting issue; or (ii) any matter that was either the subject of a
      disagreement (as defined in Item 304(a)(1)(iv) of Regulation S-K and the related instructions) or a reportable event (as described in Item 304(a)(1)(v) of Regulation S-K).</div>
